    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Nokia advances AI-ready data center networking with successful Ultra Ethernet test

We’re proud to announce a major milestone in AI infrastructure: Nokia, in collaboration with <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/keysight-technologies?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Keysight Technologies</a>, has successfully completed end-to-end testing of Ultra Ethernet Transport (UET) traffic across our 7220 IXR and 7250 IXR data center switches.
This test validates our commitment to the Ultra Ethernet Consortium (UEC) and showcases our readiness to support AI and HPC workloads with: 
✅ Ultra-low latency
✅ Zero packet loss
✅ Massive bandwidth scalability

With support for RoCEv2 and DCQCN, our portfolio is already commercially available and ready to meet the demands of modern AI data centers.

        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">It may look like a simple shipping container, but inside is a sophisticated, custom-built modular test lab where wireless networks are tested in real-world conditions. 

During her recent visit to Nokia’s new campus in Oulu, our Futurist in Residence, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/cathyhackl?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Cathy Hackl</a>, explored this lab and saw firsthand how it contributes to the innovations shaping smarter, more energy-efficient networks. 

More about the home of radio: <a class="link" href="https://nokia.ly/4gnm7fx?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://nokia.ly/4gnm7fx</a>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">My recent visit to <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/nokiabelllabs?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Nokia Bell Labs</a> left me deeply inspired. In the industrial robotics lab, I saw how AI is being developed to give robots an understanding of their physical environment enabling them to work alongside humans to boost safety, efficiency, and decision-making.

But that’s just one example. Across <a class="link" href="https://fi.linkedin.com/company/nokia?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Nokia</a>, I’ve been exploring their groundbreaking AI research that spans:

🔹 Networking for AI workloads that connects GPU clusters and data centers with ultra-low latency
🔹 AI-driven RAN and self-organizing networks that cut energy use while improving 5G performance
🔹 AI-powered cybersecurity that can predict and prevent threats in real time
🔹 Autonomous networks that sense, think and act to optimize themselves
🔹 Quantum-safe optical and IP networks built for the massive data demands of AI

It’s clear we are at the start of an AI supercycle that will reshape industries, economies, and societies as profoundly as the internet did. Nokia is showing how trusted connectivity and responsible AI can unlock these opportunities while keeping us secure and sustainable.

As Futurist in Residence with Nokia, I’m hugely excited to see these advances up close and to explore what they mean for the future. 

Over the coming weeks, I’ll be sharing a lot more content on this topic as part of our collaboration.

👉 To find out more, click here: <a class="link" href="https://nokia.ly/47GdElr?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://nokia.ly/47GdElr</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fad&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ad</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">What does it take to make closed-loop automation in telecom a reality? 

In the latest episode of Networked, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/attbusiness/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>AT&amp;T Business</a>’s <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/yigal-elbaz-b1372b1?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Yigal Elbaz</a> sits down with <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/raghavsahgal?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Raghav Sahgal</a> to discuss why moving to open, cloud-native networks is essential for enabling automation and AI-driven transformation. 

🎥 Watch the full conversation to learn why openness is the key to shaping the future of telecom: <a class="link" href="https://nokia.ly/47nDIBQ?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://nokia.ly/47nDIBQ</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Smarter. Greener. Faster. Ready for the future.  
Our research and standardization teams are designing 6G so that every signal, device, and connection uses less energy, without compromising on performance or security.  

They’re turning bold ideas into networks we can actually rely on. Experts <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/peter-vetter-a72b444?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Peter Vetter</a> and <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/peter-merz-062ab01?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Peter Merz</a> share more in their new blog: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/egnQpfiE?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/egnQpfiE</a>

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Farchitectingtomorrow&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ArchitectingTomorrow</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fnokia6g&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Nokia6G</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fbelllabs&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#BellLabs</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Building the future of enterprise AI means moving past the myths and focusing on real-world solutions. That's why we loved this video from futurist in residence, <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/bernardmarr?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Bernard Marr</a>, breaking down the key themes at Big Data LDN 2025.

Watch as he covers everything from Generative AI to modern data architecture and the critical importance of strong data governance.</p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">I was at Big Data LDN 2025 today in my role as Futurist in Residence at @Nokia. It’s one of Europe’s leading data and AI events, and three themes really stood out this year:
 
✦ Generative AI &amp; AI Agents
The conversation has moved beyond experimentation. Organisations are now exploring autonomous agents and GenAI systems that embed intelligence directly into workflows and applications.
 
✦ Data Strategy, Governance &amp; Leadership
AI success depends on clear strategy, strong governance, ethical oversight and C-level ownership. Companies are working hard to turn data and AI into real business value with the right guardrails.
 
✦ Modern Data Architecture &amp; Engineering
Real-time platforms, DataOps, observability and data-as-a-product are transforming how enterprises design and scale data systems for AI.
 
<a class="link" href="https://ca.linkedin.com/in/w-sean-kennedy?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Sean Kennedy</a>, Head of @Nokia Bell Labs AI Research, also presented a fascinating session on AI myths that hold companies back and how to move past them. I’ll be sharing more on these myths, along with other exciting things Nokia is doing in AI, over the coming weeks.
 
Which trends do you think will shape the future of data and AI?

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fad&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Ad</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fnokia&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Nokia</a></p>
